<h3 class="legacy-component-example-title">Unread and Unsaved Success Overflow Tab</h3>
<div class="legacy-component-example-preview" data-legacy-preview><div class="slds-tabs_default slds-sub-tabs">

          &lt;span class=&quot;slds-indicator-container&quot;&gt;
